 /**************************************************************/       
 /*   FORSKUD06  VURDOPL2 -> VURDOPL02                         */       
 VURDOPL02: PROC;                                                       
                                                                        
         IF CN570.VURDOPL02.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(1).EJBOLTYP < '1' &          
            CN570.VURDOPL02.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2).EJBOLTYP > '0'            
         THEN                                                           
            DO;                                                         
               CN570.VURDOPL02.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(1) =                      
               CN570.VURDOPL02.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2), BY NAME;              
               CN570.VURDOPL02.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2) = '';                  
               TV.FLYTEJB02 = TV.FLYTEJB02 + 1;                         
            END;                                                        
                                                                        
 END  VURDOPL02;                                                        
 /**************************************************************/       
 VURDOPL01: PROC;                                                       
                                                                        
         IF CN570.VURDOPL01.EJEBOL(1).EJBOLTYP < '1' & /*FORSKUD06*/    
            CN570.VURDOPL01.EJEBOL(2).EJBOLTYP > '0'   /*FORSKUD06*/    
         THEN                                                           
            DO;                                                         
               CN570.VURDOPL01.EJEBOL(1) =             /*FORSKUD06*/    
               CN570.VURDOPL01.EJEBOL(2), BY NAME;     /*FORSKUD06*/    
               CN570.VURDOPL01.EJEBOL(2) = '';         /*FORSKUD06*/    
               TV.FLYTEJB01 = TV.FLYTEJB01 + 1;        /*FORSKUD06*/    
            END;                                                        
                                                                        
 END  VURDOPL01;                                                        
 /**************************************************************/       
 SKATSTOP: PROC;                                      /*FORSKUD06*/     
                                                                        
         IF CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(1).EJEBOL(1).EJBOLTYP < '1' &        
            CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(1).EJEBOL(2).EJBOLTYP > '0'          
         THEN                                                           
            DO;                                                         
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(1).EJEBOL(1) =                    
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(1).EJEBOL(2), BY NAME;            
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(1).EJEBOL(2) = '';                
               TV.FLYTEJB071Ø = TV.FLYTEJB071Ø + 1;                     
            END;                                                        
                                                                        
         IF CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(2).EJEBOL(1).EJBOLTYP < '1' &        
            CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(2).EJEBOL(2).EJBOLTYP > '0'          
         THEN                                                           
            DO;                                                         
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(2).EJEBOL(1) =                    
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(2).EJEBOL(2), BY NAME;            
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER01(2).EJEBOL(2) = '';                
               TV.FLYTEJB071N = TV.FLYTEJB071N + 1;                     
            END;                                                        
                                                                        
         IF CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(1).EJEBOL(1).EJBOLTYP < '1' &        
            CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(1).EJEBOL(2).EJBOLTYP > '0'          
         THEN                                                           
            DO;                                                         
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(1).EJEBOL(1) =                    
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(1).EJEBOL(2), BY NAME;            
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(1).EJEBOL(2) = '';                
               TV.FLYTEJB072Ø = TV.FLYTEJB072Ø + 1;                     
            END;                                                        
                                                                        
         IF CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(2).EJEBOL(1).EJBOLTYP < '1' &        
            CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(2).EJEBOL(2).EJBOLTYP > '0'          
         THEN                                                           
            DO;                                                         
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(2).EJEBOL(1) =                    
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(2).EJEBOL(2), BY NAME;            
               CN570.SKATSTOP.OMBER02(2).EJEBOL(2) = '';                
               TV.FLYTEJB072N = TV.FLYTEJB072N + 1;                     
            END;                                                        
 END  SKATSTOP;                                                         
 /**************************************************************/       
 VURDOPLGL: PROC;                                                       
                            /*FORSKUD06   VURDOPL1 -> VURDOPLGL*/       
         IF CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.CEJERL = '0'                        
         THEN                                                           
            CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.CEJERL = ' ';                       
                                                                        
         IF CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.CUOP = '0'                          
         THEN                                                           
            CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.CUOP = ' ';                         
                                                                        
         IF CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(1).EJBOLTYP < '1' &          
            CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2).EJBOLTYP > '0'            
         THEN                                                           
            DO;                                                         
               CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(1) =                      
               CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2), BY NAME;              
               CN570.VURDOPLGL.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2) = '';                  
               TV.FLYTEJB07 = TV.FLYTEJB07 + 1;                         
            END;                                                        
                                                                        
 END  VURDOPLGL;                                                        
 /************************************************************/         
 VURDOPLNY: PROC;                                                       
               /*FORSKUD06   VURDOPL0 -> VURDOPLNY  */                  
         IF CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.CFORSKEL = '0'                      
         THEN                                                           
            CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.CFORSKEL = ' ';

         THEN                                                           
            CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.CEJERL = ' ';

         THEN                                                           
            CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.CUOP = ' ';                         
                                                                        
         IF CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(1).EJBOLTYP < '1' &          
            CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2).EJBOLTYP > '0'            
         THEN

               CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(1) =                      
               CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2), BY NAME;              
               CN570.VURDOPLNY.ÅRSVURD.EJEBOL(2) = '';                  
               TV.FLYTEJBAKT = TV.FLYTEJBAKT + 1;
